kiṃ yajñairbahubhirjāpyaiḥ kiṃ tapobhirdhanārpaṇaiḥ  /
svargamokṣapradā gaṅgā sukhasevyā yataḥ sthitā  // 2,38.39 //
yajñairyamaiśca niyamairdānaiḥ saṃnyāsato 'pi vā  /
na tatphalamavāproti gaṅgāṃ sevya yadāpnuyāt  // 2,38.40 //
prabhāse gosahastreṇa rāhugraste divākare  /
yatphalaṃ labhate martyo gaṅgāyāṃ taddinena vai  // 2,38.41 //
anyopāyāṃśca yastyaktvā mīkṣakāmaḥ suniścitaḥ  /
gaṅgātīre sukhaṃ tiṣṭhetsa vai mokṣasya bhājanam  // 2,38.42 //
vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣaṇa gaṅgā sadyastu mokṣadā  /
pratimāsaṃ caturdaśyāmaṣṭamyāṃ caiva sarvadā  // 2,38.43 //
gaṅgātīre nivāsaśca yāvajjīvaṃ ca siddhidaḥ  /
kṛcchrāṇi sarvadā kṛtvā yatphalaṃ sukhamaśnute  // 2,38.44 //
sadā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caiva tallabhejjāhnavītaṭe  /
gaṅgāsevāparasyeha divasārddhena yatphalam  // 2,38.45 //
na tacchakyaṃ brahmasute prāptuṃ kratuśatairapi  /
sarvayajñatapodānayogasvādhyāyakarmabhiḥ  // 2,38.46 //
yatphalaṃ tallabhedbhaktyā gaṅgātīranivāsataḥ  /
yatpuṇyaṃ satyavacanairnaiṣṭhikabrahmacāriṇām  // 2,38.47 //
yadagnihotriṇāṃ puṇyaṃ tattu gaṅgānivāsataḥ  /
samātṛpitṛdārāṇāṃ kulakoṭimanantakam  // 2,38.48 //
gaṅgābhaktistārayate saṃsārārṇavato dhruvam  /
saṃtoṣaḥ paramaiśvaryaṃ tattvajñānaṃ sukhātmanām  // 2,38.49 //
vinayācārasaṃpattirgaṅgābhaktasya jāyate  /
kṛtakṛtyo bhavenmartyo gaṅgāṃ prāpyaiva kevalam  // 2,38.50 //
tadbhaktastatparaśca syānmṛto vāpi na saṃśayaḥ  /
bhaktyā tajjalasaṃsparśī tajjalaṃ pibate ca yaḥ  // 2,38.51 //
anāyāsena hi naro mokṣo pāyaṃ sa vindati  /
dīkṣitaḥ sarvayajñeṣu somapānaṃ dine dine  // 2,38.52 //
sarvāṇi yaṃṣāṃ gaṅgāyāstoyaiḥ kṛtyāni sarvadā  /
dehaṃ tyaktvā narāste tu modante śivasannidhau  // 2,38.53 //
devāḥ somārkasaṃsthāni yathā śakrādayo mukhaiḥ  /
amṛtānyupabhuñjanti tathā gaṅgājalaṃ narāḥ  // 2,38.54 //
kanyādānaiśca vidhivadbhūmidānaiśca bhaktitaḥ  /
annadānaiśca godānaiḥ svarṇadānādibhistathā  // 2,38.55 //
rathāśvagajadānaiśca yatpuṇyaṃ parikīrtitam  /
tataḥ śataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ gaṅgāṃbhaśculukāśanāt  // 2,38.56 //
cāndrāyaṇasahasrāṇāṃ yatphalaṃ parikīrtitam  /
tato 'dhikaphalaṃ gaṅgātoyapānādavāpyate  // 2,38.57 //
gaṇḍūṣamātrapāne tu aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet  /
svacchandaṃ yaḥ pibedaṃbhastasya muktiḥ kare sthitā  // 2,38.58 //
tribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ saptabhistvatha yāmunam  /
nārmadaṃ daśabhirmāsairgāṅgaṃ varṣeṇa jīryati  // 2,38.59 //
śāstreṇākṛtatoyānāṃ mṛtānāṃ kvāpi dehanām  /
taduttaraphalāvāptirgaṅgāyāmasthiyogataḥ  // 2,38.60 //
cāndrāyaṇasahasraṃ tu yaścaretkāyaśodhanam  /
yaḥ pibettu yatheṣṭhaṃ hi gaṅgāmbhaḥ sa viśiṣyate  // 2,38.61 //
gaṅgāṃ paśyati yaḥ stauti snāti bhaktyā pibejjalam  /
sa svargaṃ jñānamamalaṃ yogaṃ mokṣaṃ ca vindati  // 2,38.62 //
yastu sūryyāṃśuniṣṭaptaṃ gāṅgeyaṃ pibate jalam  /
gomūtrayāvakāhārādgāṅgapānaṃ viśiṣyate  // 2,38.63 //

iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīvasusaṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmyavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


vasuruvāca
śṛṇu mohini vakṣyāmi gaṅgāyā darśane phalam  /
yaduktaṃ hi purāṇeṣu munibhistattvadarśibhiḥ  // 2,39.1 //
bhavanti nirviṣāḥ sarpā yathā tārkṣyasya daśa nāt  /
gaṅgāsaṃdarśanāttadvatsarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  // 2,39.2 //
saptāvarān saptaparān pitṛṃstebhyaśca ye pare  /
pumāṃstārayate gaṅgāṃ vīkṣya spṛṣṭvāvagāhya ca  // 2,39.3 //
darśanātsparśanātpānāttathā gaṅgeti kīrtanāt  /
pumānpunāti puruṣāñchataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ  // 2,39.4 //
jñānamaiśvaryamatulaṃ pratiṣṭhāyuryaśastathā  /
śubhānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca gaṅgādarśanajaṃ phalam  // 2,39.5 //
sarvendriyāṇāṃ cāñcalyaṃ vyasanāni ca pātakam  /
nirghṛṇatvaṃ ca naśyanti gaṅgādarśana mātrataḥ  // 2,39.6 //
parahiṃsā ca kauṭilyaṃ paradoṣādyavekṣaṇam  /
dāṃbhikatvaṃ nṛṇāṃ gaṅgādarśanādeva naśyati  // 2,39.7 //
muhurmuhustathā paśyetspṛśedvāpi muhurmuhuḥ  /
bhaktyā yadicchati naraḥ śāśvataṃ padamavyayam  // 2,39.8 //
vāpīkūpataḍāgādiprapāsatrādibhistathā  /
anyatra yadbhavetpuṇyaṃ tadgaṅgādarśanādbhavet  // 2,39.9 //
yatphalaṃ jāyate puṃsāṃ darśane paramātmanaḥ  /
tadbhavedeva gaṅgāyā darśanādbhaktibhāvataḥ  // 2,39.10 //
naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre narmadāyāṃ ca puṣkare  /
snānātsaṃsparśanā sevya yatphalaṃ labhate naraḥ  // 2,39.11 //
tadgaṅgādarśanādeva kalau prāhurmaharṣayaḥ  /
atha te smaraṇasyāpi gaṅgāyā bhūpabhāmini  // 2,39.12 //
pravakṣyāmi phalaṃ yattu purāṇeṣu prakīrtitam  /
aśubhaiḥ karmabhiryuktānmajjamānānbhavārṇave  // 2,39.13 //
patato narake gaṅgā smṛtā dūrātsamuddharet  /
yojanānāṃ sahasreṣu gaṅgāṃ smarati yo naraḥ  // 2,39.14 //
api duṣkṛtakarmā hi labhate paramāṃ gatim  /
smaraṇādeva gaṅgāyāḥ pāpasaṃghātapañjaram  // 2,39.15 //
bhedaṃ sahasradhā yāti girirvajrahato yathā  /
gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapandhyāyañjāgradbhuñjan hasan rudan  // 2,39.16 //
yaḥ smaretsatataṃ gaṅgāṃ sa ca mucyeta bandhanāt  /
sahasrayojanasthāśca gaṅgāṃ bhaktyā smaranti ye  // 2,39.17 //
gaṅgāgaṅgeti cākruśya mucyante te 'pi pātakāt  /
ye ca smaranti vai gaṅgāṃ gaṅgābhaktiparāśca ye  // 2,39.18 //
te 'pyaśeṣairmahāpāpairmucyante nātra saṃśayaḥ  /
bhavanāni vicitrāṇi vicitrābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ  // 2,39.19 //
ārogyaṃ vittrasaṃpattirgaṅgāsmaraṇañja phalam  /
manasā saṃsmaredyastu gaṅgāṃ dūrasthito naraḥ  // 2,39.20 //
cāndrāyaṇasahasrasya sa phalaṃ labhate dhruvam  /
gaṅgā gaṅgā japannāma yojanānāṃ śate sthitaḥ  // 2,39.21 //
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati  /
kīrtanānmucyate pāpāddarśanānmaṅgalaṃ labhet  // 2,39.22 //
avagāhya tathā pītvā punātyāsaptamaṃ kulam  /
saptāvaparānparānsapta saptātha parataḥ parān  // 2,39.23 //
gaṅgā tārayate puṃsāṃ prasaṃgenāpi kīrtitā  /
aśraddhayāpi gaṅgāyā yattu nāmānukīrtanam  // 2,39.24 //
karoti puṇyavāhinyāḥ so 'pi svargasya bhājanam  /
sarvāvasthāṃ gato vāpi sarvadharmavivarjitaḥ  // 2,39.25 //
gaṅgāyāḥ kīrtanenaiva śubhāṃ gatimavāpnuyāt  /
brahmahā guruhāgoghnaḥ spṛṣṭo vā sarvapātakaiḥ  // 2,39.26 //
gaṅgātoyaṃ naraḥ spṛṣṭvā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  /
kadā drakṣyāmi tāṃ gaṅgāṃ kadā snānaṃ labhe hyaham  // 2,39.27 //
iti puṃsābhilaṣitā kulānāṃ tārayecchatam  /
atha snānaphalaṃ devi gaṅgāyāḥ pravadāmi te  // 2,39.28 //
yacchrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ  /
snātasya gaṅgāsalile sadyaḥ pāpaṃ praṇaśyati  // 2,39.29 //
apūrvapuṇyaprāptiśca sadyo mohini jāyate  /
snātānāṃ śucibhistoyairgāṅgeyaiḥ prayatātmanām  // 2,39.30 //
vyuṣṭirbhavati yā puṃsāṃ na sā kratuśatairapi  /
apahatya tamastīvraṃ yathā bhātyudaye raviḥ  // 2,39.31 //
tathāpahatya pāpmānaṃ bhāti gaṅgājalokṣitaḥ  /
ekenaivāpi vidhinā snānena nṛpasundari  // 2,39.32 //
aśvamedhaphalaṃ martyo gaṅgāyāṃ labhate dhruvam  /
anekajanmasaṃbhūtaṃ puṃsaḥ pāpaṃ praṇaśyati  // 2,39.33 //
snānamātreṇa gaṅgāyāḥ sadyaḥ syātpuṇyabhājanam  /
anyasthānakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ gaṅgātīre vinaśyati  // 2,39.34 //
gaṅgātīre kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ gaṅgāsnānena naśyati  /
rātrau divā ca saṃdhyāyāṃ gaṅgāyāṃ tu prayatnataḥ  // 2,39.35 //
snātvāśvamedhajaṃ puṇyaṃ gṛhe 'pyuddhṛtatatajjalaiḥ  /
sarvatīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ sarveṣṭāyataneṣu ca  // 2,39.36 //
tatphalaṃ labhate martyo gaṅgāsnānānna saṃśayaḥ  /
mahāpātakasaṃyukto yukto vā sarvapātakaiḥ  // 2,39.37 //
gaṅgāsnānena vidhivanmucyate sarvapātakaiḥ  /
gaṅgā snānātparaṃ snānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati  // 2,39.38 //
viśeṣataḥ kaliyuge pāpaṃ harati jāhnavī  /
nihatya kāmajāndoṣānkāyavākcittasaṃbhavān  // 2,39.39 //
gaṅgāsnānena bhaktyā tu modate divi devavat  /
varṣaṃ snāti ca gaṅgāyāṃ yo naro bhaktisaṃyutaḥ  // 2,39.40 //
tasya syādvaiṣṇave loke sthitiḥ kalpaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  /
āmṛtyuṃ snāti gaṅgāyāṃ yo naro nityameva ca  // 2,39.41 //
samastapāpanimuktaḥ samastakulasaṃyutaḥ  /
samastabhogasaṃyukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate  // 2,39.42 //
parārddhadvitayaṃ yāvannātra kāryā vicāraṇā  /
gaṅgāyāṃ snāti yo martyo nairantaryeṇa nityadā  // 2,39.43 //
jīvanmuktaḥ sa cātraiva mṛto viṣṇupadaṃ vrajet  /
prātaḥsnānāddaśaguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ madhyandine smṛtam  // 2,39.44 //
sāyaṅkāle śataguṇamanantaṃ śivasannidhau  /
kapilākoṭidānāddhi gaṅgāsnānaṃ viśiṣyate  // 2,39.45 //
kurukṣetrasamā gaṅgā yatra tatrāvagāhitā  /
haridvāre prayāge ca siṃdhusaṃge phalādhikā  // 2,39.46 //
ye madīyāṃśusaṃtapte jale te snānti jāhnavi  /
te bhitvā maṇḍalaṃ yānti mokṣaṃ ceti ravervacaḥ  // 2,39.47 //
yo gṛhe sve sthito 'pi tvāṃ snāne saṃkīrtayiṣyati  /
so 'pi yāsyati nākaṃ vai ityāha varuṇaśca tām  // 2,39.48 //

iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīcarite gaṅgāsnānamāhātmyaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


vasuruvāca
atha kālaviśeṣe tu gaṅgāsnānasya te phalam  /
kīrtayiṣyāmi vāmoru sāvadhānā niśāmaya  // 2,40.1 //
nairantaryeṇa gaṅgāyā māghe snāti ca yo naraḥ  /
saśakraloke suciraṃ kālaṃ tiṣṭhetsagotrajaḥ  // 2,40.2 //
tato brahmapuraṃ yāti kalpakoṭiśatāyutaiḥ  /
nairantaryeṇa vidhivadgaṅgāyāṃ snāti yo naraḥ  // 2,40.3 //
ṣaṇmāsa mekakālāśī sakṛdevottarāyaṇe  /
so 'pi viṣṇupadaṃ yāti kulānāṃ śatamuddharan  // 2,40.4 //
saṃkrāntiṣu tu sarvāsu snātvā gaṅgājale naraḥ  /
vimānenārkavarṇena sa vrajedviṣṇumandiram  // 2,40.5 //
viṣuve 'yanasaṃkrāntau viśeṣātphalamīritam  /
tapaḥsamaṃ kārtike 'pi gaṅgāsnāne phalaṃ viduḥ  // 2,40.6 //
meṣapraveśārkakāle kārtikyāṃ vāpi mohini  /
māghasnānādhikaṃ prāhuḥ kamalāsanapūrvakāḥ  // 2,40.7 //
saṃvatsarasnānajanyaṃ phalamakṣayake tithau  /
kārtike vāpi vaiśākhe iti prāha pitā tava  // 2,40.8 //
manvādau ca yugādau yatproktaṃ gaṅgājale phalam  /
snānaina yājyavanite trimāsyāpi ca tatphalam  // 2,40.9 //
dvādaśyāṃ śravaṇarkṣe ca aṣṭabhyāṃ puṣyayogataḥ  /
ārdrāyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ gaṅgāsnānaṃ sudurlabham  // 2,40.10 //
pūrṇimā mādhave puṇyā tathā kārtikamāghayoḥ  /
amāvasyāstathaiteṣāṃ gaṅgāsnāne sudurlabhāḥ  // 2,40.11 //
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ sahasraṃ tu śataṃ syātsarvaparvasu  /
amāyāṃ ca tathāṣṭamyāṃ māghāsitadale sati  // 2,40.12 //
ardhodayaṃ tadā parvakiñcinnyūnaṃ mahodayaḥ  /
mahodaye śataguṇaṃ lakṣamarddhodaye smṛtam  // 2,40.13 //
snānaṃ gaṅgājale devi grahaṇāccandrasūryayoḥ  /
māsatrayasnānaphalaṃ phālgunāṣāḍha māsayoḥ  // 2,40.14 //
janmarkṣe tu kṛte snāne gaṅgāyāṃ bhaktibhāvataḥ  /
janmaprabhṛti pāpaṃ vai saṃcitaṃ hi vinaśyati  // 2,40.15 //
caturdaśyāṃ māghakṛṣṇe vyatīpātaśca durlabhaḥ  /
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ viśeṣeṇa vaidhṛtirjāhnavījale  // 2,40.16 //
māghaṃ sakalamevāpi naro yo vidhipūrvakam  /
aruṇodayake snāyī sa tu jātismaro bhavet  // 2,40.17 //
sarvaśāstrārthavijjñānī nīrogaśca bhavedbhruvam  /
saṃkrāntyāṃ pakṣayorante grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ  // 2,40.18 //
gaṅgāsnāto naraḥ kāmādbrahmaṇaḥ sadanaṃ labhet  /
indorlakṣaguṇaṃ proktaṃ raverdaśaguṇaṃ tataḥ  // 2,40.19 //
gaṅgātīre tu saṃprāptā indoḥ koṭī raverdaśa  /
vāruṇena samāyuktā madhau kṛṣṇā trayodaśī  /
gaṅgāyāṃ yadi labhyeta sūryagrahaśataiḥ samā  // 2,40.20 //
jyeṣṭhe māsi kṣitisutadine śuklapakṣe daśamyāṃ haste śailādavataradasau jāhnavī martyalokam  /
pāpānyasyāṃ harati hi tithau sā daśaiṣādyagaṅgā puṇyaṃ dadyādapi śataguṇaṃ vājimedhakratośca  // 2,40.21 //
mahāpātakasaṃghāni yāni pāpāni saṃti me  /
govindadvādaśīṃ prāpya tāni me hana jāhnavi  // 2,40.22 //
maghāsaṃjñena ṛkṣeṇa candraḥ saṃpūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ  /
guruṇā yāti saṃyogaṃ tanmahatvaṃ titheḥ smṛtam  // 2,40.23 //
gaṅgāyāṃ yadi labhyeta sūryagrahaśataiḥ samā  /
atha deśaviśeṣeṇa snānasya phalamucyate  // 2,40.24 //
kurukṣetrāddaśaguṇā yatra tatrāvagāhitā  /
kurukṣetrācchataguṇā yatra vindhyena saṃyutā  // 2,40.25 //
vindhyācchataguṇā proktā kāśīpuryāṃ tu jāhnavī  /
sarvatra durlabhā gaṅgā triṣu sthāneṣu cādhikā  // 2,40.26 //
gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṃgame  /
eṣu snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste 'punarbhavāḥ  // 2,40.27 //
gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte snāne puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  /
saptānāṃ rājasūyānāṃ phalaṃ syādaśvamedhayoḥ  // 2,40.28 //
uṣitvā tatra māsārddhaṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ viśvajitāṃ phalam  /
daśāyutānāṃ tu gavāṃ dānapuṇyaṃ vidurbudhāḥ  // 2,40.29 //
sarottame 'tha govindaṃ rudraṃ kanakhale sthitam  /
snātvā vāpyeṣu gaṅgāyāṃ puṇyamakṣayamāpnuyāt  // 2,40.30 //
tīrthaṃ ca saukaraṃ nāma mahāpuṇyaṃ śubhe śṛṇu  /
yasminnāvirabhūtpūrvaṃ vārāhākṛtiracyutaḥ  // 2,40.31 //
śatasyāgnicitāṃ puṇyaṃ jyotiṣṭomadvayasya ca  /
agniṣṭomasahasrasya phalamāpnoti mānavaḥ  // 2,40.32 //
tatraiva brahmaṇastīrthe jyotiṣṭomāyutasya ca  /
aśvamedhatrayasyāpi snātaḥ puṇyaṃ labhennaraḥ  // 2,40.33 //
kubjākhyaṃ tīrthamanaghaṃ yatra ca vyādhayo 'khilāḥ  /
naśyanti sarvajanmotthaṃ pātakaṃ cāpi mohini  // 2,40.34 //
atrānyatkāpilaṃ tīrthaṃ yatra snāto naraḥ śubhe  /
kapilāṣṭāyutasyāpi dānatulyaphalaṃ labhet  // 2,40.35 //
gaṅgādvāre kuśāvarte bilvake nīlaparvate  /
tīrthe kanakhale snātvā dhūtapāpo vrajeddivam  // 2,40.36 //
pavitrārthaṃ tatastīrthaṃ sarvatīrthottamottamam  /
dvayorviśvajitostatra snānātpuṇyaṃ labhennaraḥ  // 2,40.37 //
veṇīrājyaṃ tatastīrthaṃ sarayūryatra gaṅgayā  /
supuṇyayā mahāpuṇyā svasā svasreva saṃgatā  // 2,40.38 //
harerdakṣiṇapādābjakṣālanādamarāpagā  /
vāmapādodbhavā vāpi sarayūrmānasaprasūḥ  // 2,40.39 //
tīrthe tatrārcayan rudraṃ viṣṇuṃ viṣṇutvamāpnuyāt  /
pañcāśvamedhaphaladaṃ snānaṃ tatra prakīrtitam  // 2,40.40 //
tatastu gāṇḍavaṃ tīrthaṃ gaṇḍakī yatra saṃgatā  /
gosahasrasya dānaṃ ca tatra snānaṃ samaṃ dvayam  // 2,40.41 //
rāmatīrthaṃ tataḥ puṇyaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ yatra sannidhau  /
somatīrthaṃ tataḥ puṇyaṃ yatrāsau nakulo muniḥ  // 2,40.42 //
samabhyarcya śivaṃ dhyāyangaṇatāṃ tu samāyayau  /
caṃpakākhyaṃ puṇyatīrthaṃ yadgaṅgottaravāhinī  // 2,40.43 //
maṇikarṇikayā tulyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam  /
kalaśākhyaṃ tatastīrthaṃ kalaśādutthito muniḥ  // 2,40.44 //
agastyaḥ pūjayanyatra rudraṃ munivaro 'bhavat  /
somadvīpaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ tīrthaṃ vārāṇasīsamam  // 2,40.45 //
somo yatrārcayannīśaṃ rudreṇa śirasā dhṛtaḥ  /
viśvāmitrasya bhaginī gaṅgayā yatra saṃgatā  // 2,40.46 //
tatrāpluto naro bhūyādvāsavasya priyo 'tithiḥ  /
jahnuhrade mahātīrthe snāto martyo hi mohini  // 2,40.47 //
ekaviṃśatikulyānāṃ tārako bhavati dhruvam  /
tasmādadititīrthaṃ ca yatrāvāpāditirharim  // 2,40.48 //
kaśyapāttatra subhage snānamāhurmahodayam  /
śiloccayaṃ mahātīrthaṃ yatra taptvā tapaḥ prajāḥ  // 2,40.49 //
tṛṇādibhiḥ saha svargaṃ yānti tīrthagaṇāśrayāt  /
indrāṇīnāmatīrthaṃ syādyatrendrāṇī tu vāsavam  // 2,40.50 //
tapastaptvā patiṃ lebhe sevyametatprayāgavat  /
puṇyadaṃ snātakaṃ tīrthaṃ viśvāmitrastapaścaran  // 2,40.51 //
yatra brahmarṣitāṃ lebhe kṣattriyastīrthā sevayā  /
pradyumnatīrthaṃ tapasā khyātaṃ yatra smaro hareḥ  // 2,40.52 //
pradyumnanāmā putro 'bhūtparaṃ tatra mahodayam  /
tato dakṣaprayāgaṃ tu gaṅgāto yamunāgata  // 2,40.53 //
snātvā tatrākṣayaṃ puṇyaṃ prayāga iva labhyate  // 2,40.54 //

iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīvasusaṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye sthalaviśeṣasnānaphalakathanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________

vasuruvāca
athāvagāhanādīnāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalamucyate  /
sāvadhānā śṛṇuṣva tvaṃ brahmaputri nṛpapriye  // 2,41.1 //
yaiḥ puṇyavāhinī gaṅgā sakṛdbhaktyāvagāhitā  /
teṣāṃ kulānāṃ lakṣaṃ tu bhavāttārayate śivā  // 2,41.2 //
sāmānyasthānato devi tatra saṃdhyā hyupāsitā  /
puṇyaṃ lakṣaguṇaṃ kartuṃ samarthā dvijapāvanī  // 2,41.3 //
dattāḥ pitṛbhyo yatrāpastanayaiḥ śraddhayānvitaiḥ  /
akṣayāṃ tu prakurvanti tṛptiṃ mohini durlabhām  // 2,41.4 //
yāvantaśca tilā martyārgṛhītāḥ pitṛkarmaṇi  /
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi pitaraḥ svargavāsinaḥ  // 2,41.5 //
pitṛlokeṣu ye kecitsarveṣāṃ pitaraḥ sthitāḥ  /
tarpyamāṇāḥ parāṃ tṛptiṃ yānti gaṅgājalaiḥ śubhaiḥ  // 2,41.6 //
ya icchetsaphalaṃ janma saṃtatiṃ vā śubhānane  /
sa pitṝṃstarpayedgaṅgāmabhigamya surāṃstathā  // 2,41.7 //
ye matā durgatā martyāstarpitāstatkulodbhavaiḥ  /
kuśaistilairgāṅgajalaiste prayānti hareḥ padam  // 2,41.8 //
svargasasthāśca ye kecitpitaraḥ puṇyaśīlinaḥ  /
te tarpitā gāṅgajalairmokṣe yānti vidhervacaḥ  // 2,41.9 //
māsaṃ tarpaṇamātreṇa piṇḍasaṃpātanena ca  /
gaṅgāyāṃ pitaraḥ sarve suprītāḥ sūryavarcasaḥ  // 2,41.10 //
apsaro gaṇaṇasaṃyuktānhemaratnavibhūṣitān  /
muktājālaparicchannānveṇuvīṇānināditān  // 2,41.11 //
bherīśaṅkhamṛdaṅgādinirghoṣānsragvibhūṣitān  /
gandharvadeharucirāndivyabhogasamanvitān  // 2,41.12 //  //
āruhya tu vimānāgryānbrahyalokaṃ prayānti hi  /
gaṅgāyāṃ tu naraḥ snātvā yo nityaṃ liṅgamarcayet  // 2,41.13 //
ekena janmanā mokṣaṃ paramānpoti sa dhruvam  /
agnihotrāṇi vedāśca yajñāśca bahudakṣiṇāḥ  // 2,41.14 //
gaṅgāyāṃ liṅgapūjāyāḥ koṭyaṃśenāpi no samāḥ  /
pitṝnudiśya vā devāngaṅgāṃbhibhiḥ prasiṃcayet  // 2,41.15 //
tṛptāḥ syustasya pitaro narakasthāśca tatkṣaṇāt  /
mṛtkuṃbhāttāmrakuṃbhaistu snānaṃ daśaguṇaṃ smṛtam  // 2,41.16 //
raupyaiḥ śataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ hemaiḥ koṭiguṇaṃ smṛtam  /
evamarghe ca naivedye balipūjādiṣu kramāt  // 2,41.17 //
pātrāṃ taraviśeṣeṇa phalaṃ caivottarottaram  /
vibhave sati yo mohānna kuryādvidhivistaram  // 2,41.18 //
na sa tatkarmaphalabhāgdevadrohī prakīrtyate  /
devānāṃ darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ darśanātsparśanaṃ varam  // 2,41.19 //
sparśanādarcanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ ghṛtasnānamataḥ param  /
prāhurgaṅgājalaiḥ snānaṃ ghṛtasnānasamaṃ budhāḥ  // 2,41.20 //
arghyaṃ dravyaviśeṣeṇa gaṅgātoyena yaḥ sakṛt  /
māgadhaprasthamātreṇa tāmrapātrasthitena ca  // 2,41.21 //
devatābhyaḥ pradadyāttu svakīyapitṛbhiḥ saha  /
putrapautraiśca saṃyuktaḥ sa ca vai svargamāpnuyāt  /
āpaḥ kṣīraṃ kuśāgrāṇi ghṛtaṃ dadhi tathā madhu  // 2,41.22 //
raktāni karavīrāṇi tathā vai raktacandanam  /
aṣṭāṅgaireṣa yuktor'gho bhānave parikīrtitaḥ  // 2,41.23 //
viṣṇoḥ śivasya sūryyasya durgāyā brahmaṇastathā  /
gaṅgātīre pratiṣṭhāṃ tu yaḥ karoti narottamaḥ  // 2,41.24 //
tathaivāyatanānyeṣāṃ kārayatyapi śaktitaḥ  /
anyatīrtheṣu karaṇātkoṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  // 2,41.25 //
gaṅgātīrasamudbhūtamṛdā ligāni śaktitaḥ  /
salakṣaṇāni kṛtvā tu pratiṣṭhāpya dine dine  // 2,41.26 //
mantreśca patrapuṣpādyaiḥ pūjayitvā ca śaktitaḥ  /
gaṅgāyāṃ nikṣipennityaṃ tasya pupayamanantakam  // 2,41.27 //
sarvānandapradāyinyāṃ gaṅgāyāṃ yo narottamaḥ  /
aṣṭākṣaraṃ japedbhaktya muktistasya kare sthitā  // 2,41.28 //
namo nārāyaṇāyeti praṇavādyaṃ niyamya ca  /
ṣaṇmāsaṃ japataḥ sarvā hyupatiṣṭhanti siddhayaḥ  // 2,41.29 //
namaḥ śivāyeti mantraṃ satāraṃ vidhinā tu yaḥ  /
caturviśatilakṣaṃ vai japetsākṣātsaśaṅkaraḥ  // 2,41.30 //
pañcākṣarī siddhavidyā śiva eva na saṃśayaḥ  /
apavitraḥ pavitro vā japanniṣpātako bhavet  // 2,41.31 //
pūjitāyāṃ tu gaṅgāyāṃ pūjitāḥ sarva devatāḥ  /
tasmātsarvaprayatnena pūjayedamarāpagām  // 2,41.32 //
caturbhujāṃ trinetrāṃ ca sarvāvayavaśobhitām  /
ratnakuṃbhasitāṃbhojavarābhayakaraṃ śubhām  // 2,41.33 //
śvetavastraparīdhānāṃ muktāmaṇivibhūṣitām  /
suprasannāṃ suvadanāṃ karuṇārdrahṛdaṃbujām  // 2,41.34 //
sudhāplāvitabhūpṛṣṭhāṃ trailokyanamitāṃ sadā  /
dhyātvā jalamayīṃ gaṅgāṃ pūjayanpuṇyabhāgbhavet  // 2,41.35 //
māsārddhamapi yastvevaṃ nairantaryeṇa pūjayet  /
sa eva devasadṛśo bahukāle phalādhikaḥ  // 2,41.36 //
vaiśākhaśuklasaptamyāṃ jahnunā jāhnavī purā  /
krodhātpītā punastyaktā karṇaraṅghrāttu dakṣiṇāt  // 2,41.37 //
tāṃ tatra pūjayeddevīṃ gaṅgāṃ gaganamekhalām  /
akṣayāyāṃ tu vaiśākhe kārtike 'pi śubhānane  // 2,41.38 //
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā yavānnaiśca tilaistathā  /
viṣṇuṃ gaṅgāṃ ca śaṃbhuṃ ca pūjayedbhakti bhāvataḥ  // 2,41.39 //
tathā sugandhaiḥ kusumaiḥ kuṅkumāgarumandanaiḥ  /
tulasībilvapatrādyairmātuluṅgaphalādibhiḥ  // 2,41.40 //
dhūpairdīpaiśca naivedyairyathā vibhavavistaraiḥ  /
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca  // 2,41.41 //
divyaṃ vimānamāsthāya viṣṇuloke mahīyate  /
tato mahītalaṃ prāpya rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ  // 2,41.42 //
bhuktvā vividhasaukhyāni rūpaśīlaguṇānvitaḥ  /
dehānte jñānavānbhūtvā śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt  // 2,41.43 //
yajño dānaṃ tapo japyaṃ śrāddhaṃ ca surapūjanam  /
gaṅgāyāṃ tu kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ bhavet  // 2,41.44 //
yastvakṣayatṛtīyāyāṃ gaṅgātīre dadāti vai  /
ghṛtadhenuṃ vidhānena tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu  // 2,41.45 //
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca  /
sahasrādityasaṃkāśaḥ sarvakāmasamanvitaḥ  // 2,41.46 //
hemaratna maye citre vimāne haṃsabhūṣite  /
svakīyapitṛbhiḥ sārddhaṃ brahmaloke mahīyate  // 2,41.47 //
tatastu jāyate vipro gaṅgātīre dhanānvitaḥ  /
ante tu brahmavidbhūtvā mokṣamāpnotyasaṃśayaḥ  // 2,41.48 //
tathaiva gopradānaṃ ca vidhinā kurute tu yaḥ  /
golomasaṃkhyavarṣāṇi svargaloke mahīyate  // 2,41.49 //
jāyate ca kule paścāddhanadhānyasamākule  /
ratnakāñcanabhūpūrṇe śīlavidyāyaśonvite  // 2,41.50 //
sa bhuktvā vipulānbhogānputrapautrasamanvitaḥ  /
mokṣabhāgī bhavennṛnaṃ nātrakāryā vicāraṇā  // 2,41.51 //
kapilā yadi dattā syādvidhinā vedapārage  /
narakasthānpitṝnsarvānsvargaṃ nayati vai tadā  // 2,41.52 //
bhūmiṃ nivartanamitāṃ gaṅgātīre dadāti yaḥ  /
bhūmireṇupramāṇābdaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātigaḥ  // 2,41.53 //
jāyate ca punarbhūmau saptadvīpapatirbhavet  /
bherīśaṅkhādinirghoṣairgītavāditraniḥsvanaiḥ  // 2,41.54 //
stutibhirmāgaghānāṃ ca supto 'sau pratibudhyate  /
sarvasaukhyānyavāpyeha sarvadharmaparāyaṇaḥ  // 2,41.55 //
narakasthānpitṝnsarvānprāpayitvā divaṃ tathā  /
svargasthitānmokṣayitvā svayaṃ jñānī ca mohini  // 2,41.56 //
ante jñānāsinā chitvā avidyāṃ pañcaparvikām  /
paraṃ vairāgyamāpannaḥ paraṃ brahmādhi gacchati  // 2,41.57 //
saptahastena daṇḍena triṃśaddaṇḍā nivartanam  /
tribhāgahīnaṃ gocarma mānamāha vidhiḥ svayam  // 2,41.58 //
grāmaṃ gaṅgātaṭe yo vai brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati  /
brahmaviṣṇuśivaprītye durgāyā bhāskarasya ca  // 2,41.59 //
sarvadāneṣu yatpuṇyaṃ sarvayajñeṣu yatphalam  /
tapovrateṣu puṇyeṣu yatphalaṃ parikīrtitam  // 2,41.60 //
sahasraguṇitaṃ tattu vijñeyaṃ grāmadāyinaḥ  /
sūryakoṭipratīkāśe vimāne vaiṣṇave pure  // 2,41.61 //
krīḍate śāṅkare vāpi stuto devādibhirmudā  /
bhūmireṇvabdasaṃkhyākaṃ kālaṃ sthitvā ca tatra saḥ  // 2,41.62 //
aṇimādiguṇairyukte yogināṃ jāyate kule  /
akṣayāyāṃ tu yo devi svarṇaṃ ṣoḍaśamāsikam  // 2,41.63 //
dadāti dvijamukhyāya so 'pi lokeṣu pūjyate  /
annadānādviṣṇulokaṃ śaivaṃ vai tiladānataḥ  // 2,41.64 //
brāhmaṃ ratnapradānena gohiraṇyena vāsavam  /
gāndharvaṃ svarṇavāsobhiḥ kīrtiṃ kanyāpradānataḥ  // 2,41.65 //
vidyayā muktidaṃ jñānaṃ prāpya yāyānnirañjanam  /
gaṃmātīre naro yastu nānāvṛkṣaiḥ samanvitam  // 2,41.66 //
ārāmaṃ kārayedbhaktyā gṛhaṃ copavanānvitam  /
kadalīnārikeraiśca kapitthāśokacaṃpakaiḥ  // 2,41.67 //
panasairbilvavṛkṣaiśca kadaṃbāśvatthapāṭalaiḥ  /
āmraistālairnāgaraṅgairvṛkṣairanyaiśca saṃyutam  // 2,41.68 //
jātīvijayasaṃyuktaṃ tathā pāṭalarājitam  /
nicitaṃ kārayitvaivamāvāsaṃ puṣpaśobhitam  // 2,41.69 //
śivāya viṣṇave vāpi durgāyai bhāskarāya ca  /
prayacchati tathā bhaktyā sarvārthaṃ parikalpya ca  // 2,41.70 //
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vakṣye saṃkṣepānnatu vistarāt  /
yāvanti teṣāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ puṣpamūlaphalāni ca  // 2,41.71 //
bījāni ca vicitrāṇi teṣāṃ mūlāni vai tathā  /
tāvatkalpasahasrāṇi teṣāṃ lokeṣu saṃsthitiḥ  // 2,41.72 //

iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīvasusaṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye dānādividhivarṇanaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________

mohinyuvāca
dhanyāhaṃ kṛtakṛtyāhaṃ saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ mama  /
yacchrutaṃ tvanmukhāṃbhojādgāmāhātmyamuttamam  // 2,42.1 //
aho gaṅgāsamaṃ tīrthaṃ nāsti kiñciddharā tale  /
yasyāḥ saṃdarśanādīnāmīdṛśaṃ puṇyamīritam  // 2,42.2 //
guḍadhenvādidhenūnāṃ vidhānaṃ ca yathākramam  /
tathā kathayaviprendra bhaktāhaṃ tava sarvadā  // 2,42.3 //
vasiṣṭha uvāca
tacchrutvā mohinīvākyaṃ vasustasyāḥ purohitaḥ  /
vedāgamānāṃ tattvajñaḥ smayamāna uvāca ha  // 2,42.4 //
vasuruvāca
śṛṇu mohini vakṣyāmi yatpṛṣṭaṃ hi tvayā mama  /
guḍadhenuvidhānaṃ ca yathā śāstre prakīrtitam  // 2,42.5 //
kṛṣṇājinaṃ caturgrīvaṃ vinyasedbhuvi  /
gomayenopaliptāyāṃ kuśānāstīrya yatnataḥ  // 2,42.6 //
praṅmukhīṃ kalpayeddhenumudakpādāṃ savatsakām  /
uttamā guḍadhenustu caturbhāraiḥ prakīrtitā  // 2,42.7 //
vatsaṃ bhāreṇa kurvīta bhārābhyāṃ madhyamā smṛtā  /
arddhabhāreṇa vatsaḥ syātkaniṣṭhā bhārakeṇa tu  // 2,42.8 //
caturthāṃśena vatsaḥ syād gṛhavittānusārataḥ  /
prabhuḥ prathamakalpasya yo 'nukalpena vartayet  // 2,42.9 //
na sāṃparāyikaṃ tasya durmaterjāyate phalam  /
dhenuvatsau ghṛtasyaitau sitaślakṣṇāṃbarāvṛtau  // 2,42.10 //
śuktikarṇāvikṣupādau śuddhamuktālekṣaṇau  /
sitasūtraśirālau ca sitakaṃbalakaṃbalau  // 2,42.11 //
tāmragaṇḍūkapṛṣṭhau tau sitacāmaralomakau  /
vidrumakramago petau navanītastanānvitau  // 2,42.12 //
kāṃsyadohāvindranīlamaṇikalpitatārakau  /
suvarṇaśṛṅgābharaṇau śuddharaupyakhurāvubhau  // 2,42.13 //
nānāphalaṃ samāyuktau ghrāṇagandhakaraṇḍakau  /
ityevaṃ racayitvā tu dhūpadīpairathārcayet  // 2,42.14 //
yā lakṣmīḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yā ca deveṣvavasthitā  /
dhenurūpeṇa sā devī mama śāntiṃ prayacchatu  // 2,42.15 //
dehasthā yā ca rudrāṇāṃ śaṅkarasya sadā priyā  /
dhenurūpeṇa sā devī mama pāpaṃ vyapohatu  // 2,42.16 //
viṣṇorvakṣasi yā lakṣmīḥ svāhārūpā vibhāvasoḥ  /
candrārkaśakraśaktiryā dhenurūpāstu sā śriye  // 2,42.17 //
caturmukhasya yā lakṣmīrlakṣmīryā dhanadasya ca  /
lakṣmīryā lokapālānāṃ sā dhenurvaradāstu me  // 2,42.18 //
svadhā yā pitṛmukhyānāṃ svāhā yajñamujā ca yā  /
sarvapāpaharā dhenuḥ sā me śāntiṃ prayacchatu  // 2,42.19 //
evamāṃmatrya tāṃ dhenuṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet  /
vidhānametaddhenūnāṃ sarvāsāmiha paṭhyate  // 2,42.20 //
yāstu pāparvināśinyaḥ kīrtitā daśadhenavaḥ  /
tāsāṃ svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi śāstrokaṃ śṛṇu mohini  // 2,42.21 //
prathamā guḍadhenuḥ syād ghṛtadhenurathāparā  /
tiladhenustṛtīyā ca caturthī jalasaṃjñitā  // 2,42.22 //
pañcamī kṣīradhenuśca ṣaṣṭhī madhumayī smṛtā  /
saptamī śarkarādhenurdadhidhenustathāṣṭamī  // 2,42.23 //
ratnadhenuśca navamī daśamī tu svarūpataḥ  /
kuṃbhāḥ syurdravadhenūnāṃ cetarāsāṃ tu rāśayaḥ  // 2,42.24 //
survaṇadhenumapyatra kecidicchanti sūrayaḥ  /
navanītena tailena tathā ke 'pi maharṣayaḥ  // 2,42.25 //
etadeva vidhānaṃ syādeta eva hyupaskarāḥ  /
mantrāvāhanasaṃyuktāḥ sadā parvaṇi parvaṇi  // 2,42.26 //
yathāśraddhaṃ pradātavyā bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ  /
anekayajñaphaladāḥ sarvapāpaharāḥ śubhāḥ  // 2,42.27 //
ayane viṣuve puṇye vyatīpāte 'thavā punaḥ  /
yugādau caiva manvādau coparāgādiparvasu  // 2,42.28 //
guḍadhenvādayo deyā bhaktiśraddhāsamanvitaiḥ  /
tīrtheṣu svagṛhe vāpi gaṅgātīre viśeṣataḥ  // 2,42.29 //
evaṃ datvā vidhānena dhenuṃ dvijavarāya ca  /
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya vipraṃ dakṣiṇābhiḥ pratoṣya ca  // 2,42.30 //
ṛtvijaḥ prītisaṃyukto namaskṛtya visarjayet  /
tataḥ saṃpūjayedgaṅgāṃ vidhinā susamāhitaḥ  // 2,42.31 //
aṣṭamūrtidharāṃ devīṃ divyarūpāṃ nirīkṣya ca  /
śālitandulaprasthena dviprasthapayasā tathā  // 2,42.32 //
pāyasaṃ kārayitvā ca datvā madhu ghṛtaṃ tathā  /
pratyekaṃ palamātraṃ ca bhaktibhāvena saṃyutaḥ  // 2,42.33 //
tatpāyasamapūpāṃśca modakā maṇḍalāni ca  /
tathā guñjārddhamātraṃ ca suvarṇaṃ rūpyameva ca  // 2,42.34 //
candanāgarukarpūrakuṅkumāni ca guggulam  /
bilvapatrāṇi dūrvāśca rocanā sitacandanam  // 2,42.35 //
nīlotpalāni cānyāni puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca  /
yathāśakti mahābhaktyā gaṅgāyāṃ caiva nikṣipet  // 2,42.36 //
mantreṇānena subhage purāṇoktena cāpi hi  /
oṅgaṅgāyai nārāyaṇyai śivāyai ca namonamaḥ  // 2,42.37 //
etadeva vidhānaṃ tu māsi māsi ca mohini  /
paurṇamāsyāmapāyāṃ vā kāryaṃ prātaḥ samāhitaiḥ  // 2,42.38 //
varṣaṃ yastu naro bhaktyā yathā śaktyarcayanmudā  /
haviṣyāśī mitāhāro brahmacaryasamanvitaḥ  // 2,42.39 //
dine vāpi tathā rātrā niyamena ca mohini  /
saṃvatsarānte tasyeṣā gaṅgā divyavapurddharā  // 2,42.40 //
divyamālyāṃbarā caiva divyaratnavibhūṣitā  /
pratyakṣarūpā puratastiṣṭatyeva varapradā  // 2,42.41 //
evaṃ pratyakṣarūpāṃ tāṃ gaṅgāṃ divyavapurddharām  /
dṛṣṭvā sva cakṣuṣā martyaḥ kṛtakṛtyo bhavecchubhe  // 2,42.42 //
yānyānkāmayate martyaḥ kāmāṃstāṃstānavāpnuyāt  /
niṣkāmastu labhenmokṣaṃ viprastenaiva janmanā  // 2,42.43 //
etaddhidhānaṃ ca mayoditaṃ te pṛṣṭaṃ hi sarvaṃ guḍadhenupūrvam  /
gaṅgārcanaṃ muktikaraṃ vrataṃ tta sāṃvatsaraṃ śrīpatituṣṭidaṃ hi  // 2,42.44 //

iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīvasusaṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye guḍadhenuvidhikathanaṃ nāma dvicatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ


_____________________________________________________________


vasiṣṭha uvāca
vasorvacanamākarṇya gaṅgāmāhātmyasūcakam  /
punaḥ papraccha rājendraṃ taṃ vipraṃ svapurohitam  // 2,43.1 //
mohinyuvāca
śrutaṃ vipra mayā sarvaṃ godānādi śubhāvaham  /
adhunā śrotumicchāmi gaṅgāvratamanuttamam  // 2,43.2 //
gaṅgādīnāṃ pūjanaṃ ca sthāpanaṃ tatra vā dvija  /
kiṃ phalaṃ vada sarvajña tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā  // 2,43.3 //
adhunā gatidātā tvaṃ varjitāyāśca bandhubhiḥ  /
patyā virahitā cāhaṃ putrahīnā vidāṃvara  // 2,43.4 //
tvāmeva śaraṇaṃ prāptā piturvacanagauravāt  /
tadbhavānpraṇatāyā me gaṅgāmāhātmyaṃsaṃyutam  /
devatārādhanaṃ brūhi yacchrutvā mucyate hyaghāt  // 2,43.5 //
vasiṣṭha uvāca
tacchrutvā mohinīvākyaṃ vasurvipraḥ pratāpavān  /
sabhājya mohinīṃ bhūpa prāha vedavidāṃ varaḥ  // 2,43.6 //
vasuruvāca
sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā devi lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā  // 2,43.7 //
gaṅgāmāhātmyamakhilaṃ mahāpāpapraṇāśanam  /
vṛṣadhvajena kathitaṃ śivena dayayā purā  // 2,43.8 //
prītyā devyābhi pṛṣṭena gaṅgātīranivāsinā  /
devaistu bhuktaṃ pūrvāhṇe madhyāhne ṛṣibhistathā  // 2,43.9 //
aparāhṇe ca pitṛbhiḥ śarvarṃyāṃ guhyakādibhaiḥ  /
sarvā velā atikramya naktabhojanamuttamam  // 2,43.10 //
upavāsādvāraṃ bhaikṣyaṃ bhaikṣyādvaramayācitam  /
ayācitādvāraṃ naktaṃ tasmānnaktaṃ samācaret  // 2,43.11 //
haviṣyabhojanaṃ snānaṃ satyamāhāralāghavam  /
agnikāryyamadhaḥśayyāṃ naktāśī ṣaṭ samācaret  // 2,43.12 //
gaṅgātīre māghamāse yaḥ kuryānnaktabhojanam  /
śivāyatanapārśve tu kṛśaraṃ ghṛtasaṃyutam  // 2,43.13 //
naivedyaṃ ca nivedyaiva kṛśarānnaṃ śivasya tu  /
kāṣṭhamaunena bhuñjāno jihvālaulyaṃ vivarjayet  // 2,43.14 //
palāśapatre bhuñjānaḥ śivaṃ smṛtvā jitendriyaḥ  /
dharmarājasya devyāśca pṛthakpiṇḍaṃ prakalpayet  // 2,43.15 //
sopavāsaścaturddaśyāṃ bhavedubhayapakṣayoḥ  /
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu gandhaiśca gaṅgāyāḥ salilaistathā  // 2,43.16 //
śivaṃ saṃsnāpya payasā madhvājyadadhibhiḥ pṛthak  /
tathaiva hemapuṣpaṃ ca liṅgamūrdhni vinikṣipet  // 2,43.17 //
tato dadyāttu śaktyaivāpūpañca ghṛtapācitam  /
tilāḍhakaṃ pragṛhyātha śivaliṅgopari kṣipet  // 2,43.18 //
nīlotpalaiśca sarveśaṃ pūjayetpaṅkajairapi  /
tadalābhe tu sauvarṇaiḥ paṅkajaiḥ pūjayeddharam  // 2,43.19 //
pāyasaṃ cātra madhvaktaṃ ghṛtayuktaṃ ca guggulam  /
ghṛtadīpaṃ tathā caiva candanādyairvilepanam  // 2,43.20 //
dadyādbhaktyā maheśāya tathā patraphalāni ca  /
kṛṣṇagomithunaṃ caiva sarūpaṃ ca nivedayet  // 2,43.21 //
bhojayedbrāhmaṇānaṣṭau māsāṃte tu sadakṣiṇān  /
varjayenmadhu māṃsaṃ ca taṃ māsaṃ brahmacaryavān  // 2,43.22 //
evaṃ kṛtvā yathoddiṣṭamekavāramidaṃ vratam  /
yamaiśca niyamairyuktaḥ śraddhābhaktiparāyaṇaḥ  // 2,43.23 //
iha bhogānavāpnoti pretya cānuttamāṃ gatim  /
indranīlapratīkāśairvimānaiḥ śikhisaṃyuktaiḥ  // 2,43.24 //
divyaratnamayaiścaiva divyabhogasamanvitaiḥ  /
gatvā śivapuraṃ ramyaṃ sarvasvakulasaṃyutaḥ  // 2,43.25 //
suhṛdbhirvividhaiścaiva vividhānapyabhīpsitān  /
bhuktvā bhogānaśeṣāṃśca yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam  // 2,43.26 //
tato bhavati dharmātmā jaṃbūdvīpapatistathā  /
tatra bhuṅkte samastāṃśca bhogānvigatakalmaṣaḥ  // 2,43.27 //
surūpaḥ subhagaścaiva tathā vihitaśāsanaḥ  /
sarvarogavinirmuktaḥ so 'pyetatphalabhāgbhavet  // 2,43.28 //
vaiśākhe śuklapakṣe vā caturdaśyāṃ samāhitaḥ  /
śālyannaṃ kṣīrasaṃyuktaṃ yaḥ kuryānnaktabhojanam  // 2,43.29 //
śivaṃ saṃpūjya puṣpādyairbhojyaṃ tu saṃnivedya ca  /
kāṣṭhamaunena bhuñjāno vaṭakāṣṭena vai tathā  // 2,43.30 //
maunena prayato bhūtvā kuryādvai dantadhāvanam  /
śivaliṅgasamīpe tu gaṅgātīre niśi svapet  // 2,43.31 //
paurṇamāsyāṃ prabhāte tu gaṅgāyāṃ vidhinā tathā  /
snātvopavāsaṃ saṃkalpya kuryyājjāgaraṇaṃ niśi  // 2,43.32 //
liṅgaṃ ghṛtena saṃsnāpya puṣpagandhādibhistathā  /
naivedyadhūpadīpaiśca saṃpūjya vṛṣabhaṃ śubham  // 2,43.33 //
suśvetapuṣpavastrādyairhāridraiścandanaistathā  /
alaṅkṛtya vidhānena śivāya vinivedayet  // 2,43.34 //
brāhmaṇāṃśca yathāśakti pāyasena tu bhojayet  /
evaṃ sakṛcca yo bhaktyā karoti śraddhayānvitaḥ  // 2,43.35 //
labhate daivapādonayugānāṃ dvisahasrakam  /
tapaḥ kṛtvā tu niyamādyatpuṇyaṃ tadasaṃśayam  // 2,43.36 //
haṃsakundaprabhāyuktairvimānaiścandrasannibhaiḥ  /
suśvetavṛṣayuktaiśca muktājālavibhūṣitaiḥ  // 2,43.37 //
svakīyapitṛbhiḥ sārddhaṃ prayātīśvaramandiram  /
nīlotpalasuṃgandhābhiḥ surūpābhiḥ samantataḥ  // 2,43.38 //
kāntābhirdivyarūpābhirbhuktvā bhogānanekaśaḥ  /
anantakālamaiśvaryayukto bhūtvā tato bhuvi  // 2,43.39 //
jāyate sa mahīpālaḥ kīrtyaiśvaryasamanvitaḥ  /
ekacchatreṇa sa mahīṃ pālayatyājñayā saha  // 2,43.40 //
ante vairāgyasaṃpanno gaṅgāṃ sa labhate punaḥ  /
sa tayā śraddhayā yukto gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇaṃ labhet  // 2,43.41 //
tathā tatra smṛtiṃ labdhvā mokṣamāpnoti sa dhruvam  /
jyeṣṭhe māsi site pakṣe daśamyāṃ hastasaṃyute  // 2,43.42 //
gaṅgātīre tu puruṣo nārī vā bhaktibhāvataḥ  /
niśāyāṃ jāgaraṃ kṛtvā gaṅgāṃ daśavidhaistataḥ  // 2,43.43 //
puṣpairgandhaiśca naivedyaiḥ phalaiśca daśasaṃkhyāyā  /
tathaiva dīpaistāṃbūlaiḥ pūjayecchraddhayānvitaḥ  // 2,43.44 //
snātvā bhaktyā tu jāhnavyāṃ daśakṛtvo vidhānataḥ  /
daśaprasṛti kṛṣṇaṃśca tilānsarpiśca vai jale  // 2,43.45 //
saktupiṇḍānguḍapiṇḍāndadyācca daśasaṃkhyayā  /
tato gaṅgātaṭe ramye hemnā rūpyeṇa vā tathā  // 2,43.46 //
gaṅgāyāḥ pratimāṃ kṛtvā vakṣyamāṇasvarūpiṇīm  /
padmasvastikacihnasya saṃsthitasya tathopari  // 2,43.47 //
vastrasragdāmakaṇṭhasya pūrṇakuṃbhasya copari  /
saṃsthāpya pūjayeddevīṃ tadalābhe mṛdādi vā  // 2,43.48 //
atha tatrāpyaśaktaścellikhetpiṣṭena vai bhuvi  /
caturbhujāṃ sunetrāṃ ca candrāyutasamaprabhām  // 2,43.49 //
cāmarairvījyamānāṃ ca śvetacchatropaśibhitām  /
suprasannāṃ ca varadāṃ karuṇārdranijāntarām  // 2,43.50 //
sudhāplāvitabhūpṛṣṭhāṃ devādibhirabhiṣṭutām  /
divyaratnaparītāṃ ca diṃvyamālyānulepanām  // 2,43.51 //
dhyātvā jale yathāproktāṃ tatrārcāyāṃ tu pūjayet  /
vakṣyamāṇena mantreṇa kuryātpūjāṃ viśeṣataḥ  // 2,43.52 //
pañcāmṛtena ca snānamarcāyāṃ tu viśiṣyate  /
pratimāgre sthaṇḍile tu gomayenopalepayet  // 2,43.53 //
nārāyaṇaṃ maheśaṃ ca brahmāṇaṃ bhāskaraṃ tathā  /
bhagīrathaṃ ca nṛpatiṃ himavantaṃ nageśvaram  // 2,43.54 //
gandhapuṣpādibhiścaiva yathāśakti prapūjayet  /
daśaprasthāṃ stilāndadyāddaśa viprebhya eva ca  // 2,43.55 //
daśaprasthānyavāndadyāddaśa gavyairyathāhitān  /
matsyakacchapamaṇḍūkamarādijalecarān  // 2,43.56 //
kāritānvai yathāśakti svarṇena rajatena vā  /
tadalābhe piṣṭamayānabhyarcya kusumādibhiḥ  /
gaṅgāyāṃ prakṣipetpūrvvaṃ mantreṇaiva tu mantravit  // 2,43.57 //
rathayātrādine tasminvibhave sati kārayet  /
rathārūḍhapratikṛtiṃ gaṅgāyāstūttarāmukhām  // 2,43.58 //
bhramantyā darśanaṃ loke durlabhaṃ pāpakarmaṇām  /
durgāyā rathayātrāsti tathaivātrāpi kārayet  // 2,43.59 //
evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānena vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  /
daśapāpairvakṣyamāṇaiḥ sadya eva vimucyate  // 2,43.60 //
adattānāmupādānaṃ hiṃsā caivāvidhānataḥ  /
paradāropasevā ca kāyikaṃ tribidhaṃ smṛtam  // 2,43.61 //
pāṃruṣyamanṛtaṃ vāpi paiśunyaṃ cāpi sarvaśaḥ  /
asaṃbaddhapralāpaśca vācikaṃ syāccaturvidham  // 2,43.62 //
paradravyeṣvabhidhyānaṃ manasāniṣṭacintanam  /
vitathābhiniveśaśca mānasaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam  // 2,43.63 //
etairdaśavidhaiḥ pāpaiḥ koṭijanmasamudbhavaiḥ  /
mucyate nātra saṃdeho brahmaṇo vacanaṃ yathā  // 2,43.64 //
daśa triṃśacca tānpūrvānpitṝneva tathāparān  /
uddharatyeva saṃsārānmantreṇānena pūjitā  // 2,43.65 //
oṃ namo daśaharāyai nārāyaṇyai gaṅgāyai namaḥ  /
iti mantreṇa yo martyo dine tasmindivāniśam  // 2,43.66 //
japetpacasahasrāṇi daśadharmaphalaṃ labhet  /
uddareddaśa pūrvāṇi parāṇi ca bhavārṇavāt  // 2,43.67 //
vakṣyamāṇamidaṃ stotraṃ vidhinā pratigṛhya ca  /
gaṅgāgre taddine japyaṃ viṣṇupūjāṃ pravartayet  // 2,43.68 //
oṃ namaḥ śivāyai gaṅgāyai śivadāyai namo 'stu te  /
namo 'stu viṣṇurūpiṇyai gaṅgāyai te namo namaḥ  // 2,43.69 //
sarvadevasvarūpiṇyai namo bheṣajamūrtaye  /
sarvasya sarvavyādhīnāṃ bhiṣakśreṣṭhe namo 'stu te  // 2,43.70 //
sthāṇujaṅgamasaṃbhūtaviṣahantri namo 'stu te  /
saṃsāraviṣanāśinyai jīvanāyai namonamaḥ  // 2,43.71 //
tāpatritayahantryai ca prāṇeśvaryai namonamaḥ  /
śāntyai saṃtāpahāriṇyai namaste sarvamūrtaye  // 2,43.72 //
sarvasaṃśuddhikāriṇyai namaḥ pāpavimuktaye  /
bhuktimuktipradāyinyai bhogavatyai namonamaḥ  // 2,43.73 //
mandākinyai namaste 'stu svargadāyai namonamaḥ  /
namastrailokyamūrtāyai tridaśāyai namonamaḥ  // 2,43.74 //
namaste śuklasaṃsthāyai kṣemavatyai namonamaḥ  /
tridaśāsanasaṃsthāyai tejovatyai namo 'stu te  // 2,43.75 //
mandāyai liṅgadhāriṇyai nārāyaṇyai namonamaḥ  /
namaste viśvamitrāyai revatyai te namonamaḥ  // 2,43.76 //
bṛhatyai te namo nityaṃ lokadhātryai namonamaḥ  /
namaste viśvamukhyāyai nandinyai te namonamaḥ  // 2,43.77 //
pṛthvyai śivāmṛtāyai ca virajāyai namonamaḥ  /
parāvaragatādyaiyai tārāyai te namonamaḥ  // 2,43.78 //
namaste svargasaṃsthāyai abhinnāyai namonamaḥ  /
śāntāyai te pratiṣṭhāyai varadāyai namonamaḥ  // 2,43.79 //
ugrāyai nukhajalpāyai saṃjīvinyai namonamaḥ  /
brahmagāyai brahmadāyai duritaghnyai namonamaḥ  // 2,43.80 //
praṇatārtiprabhañjinyai jaganmātre namonamaḥ  /
viluṣāyai durgahantryai dakṣāyai te namonamaḥ  // 2,43.81 //
sarvāpatpratipakṣāyai maṅgalāyai namonamaḥ  /
parāpare pare tubhya namo mokṣaprade sadā  /
gaṅgā mamāgrato bhūyādgaṅgā me pārśvayostathā  // 2,43.82 //
gaṅgā me sarvato bhūyāttvayi gaṅge 'stu me sthitiḥ  /
ādau tvamante madhye ca sarvā tvaṃ gāṅgate śive  // 2,43.83 //
tvameva mūlaprakṛtistvaṃ hi nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  /
gaṅge tvaṃ paramātmā ca śivastubhyaṃ namonamaḥ  // 2,43.84 //
itīdaṃ paṭhati stotraṃ nityaṃ bhaktiparastu yaḥ  /
śṛṇoti śraddhayā vāpi kāyavācikasaṃbhavaiḥ  // 2,43.85 //
daśadhā saṃsthitairdeṣaiḥ sarvaireva pramucyate  /
rogī pramucyate rogānmucyetāpanna āpadaḥ  // 2,43.86 //
dviṣabhdyo bandhanāccāpi bhayebhyaśca vimucyate  /
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti pretya brahmaṇi līyate  // 2,43.87 //
idaṃ stotraṃ gṛhe yasya likhitaṃ paripūjyate  /
nāgnicaurabhayaṃ tatra pāpebhyo 'pi bhayaṃ nahi  // 2,43.88 //
tasyāṃ daśamyāmetacca stotraṃ gaṅgājale sthitaḥ  /
japaṃstu daśakṛtvaśca daridro vāpi cākṣamaḥ  // 2,43.89 //
so 'pi tatphalamāpnoti gaṅgāṃ saṃpūjya bhaktitaḥ  /
pūrvoktena vidhānena phalaṃ yatparikīrtitam  // 2,43.90 //
yathā gaurī tathā gaṅgā tasmādgauryāstu pūjane  /
vidhiryo vihitaḥ samyakso 'pi gaṅgāprapūjane  // 2,43.91 //
yathā śivastathā viṣṇuryathā viṣṇustathā hyumā  /
umā yathā tathā gaṅgā cātra bhedo na vidyate  // 2,43.92 //
viṣṇurudrāntaraṃ yaśca gagāgauryantaraṃ tathā  /
lakṣmīgauryataraṃ yaśca prabrūte mūḍhadhīstu saḥ  // 2,43.93 //
śuklapakṣe divā bhūmau gaṅgāyāmuttarāyaṇe  /
dhanyā dehaṃ vimuñcanti hṛdayasthe janārdane  // 2,43.94 //
ye muñcanti narā-prāṇān gaṅgāyāṃ vidhinaṃ dini  /
te viṣṇulokaṃ gacchanti stūyamānā divisthitaiḥ  // 2,43.95 //
arddhodakena jāhnavyāṃ mniyate 'naśanena yaḥ  /
sa yāti na punarjanma brahmasāyujyameti ca  // 2,43.96 //
yā gatiryogayuktasya sātvikasya manīṣiṇaḥ  /
sā getistyajataḥ prāṇān gaṅgāyāṃ tu śarīriṇaḥ  // 2,43.97 //
anaśanaṃ gṛhītvā yo gaṅgātīre mṛto naraḥ  /
satyameva paraṃ lokamāpnoti pitṛbhiḥ saha  // 2,43.98 //
gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇātprāṇānyoḥ prājñastyaktumicchati  /
gatāni bahujanmāni yatra yatra mṛtāni ca  // 2,43.99 //
mahāṃścāpi gataḥ kālo yatra tatrāpi gacchataḥ  /
atradūre samīpe ca sadṛśaṃ yojanadvayam  // 2,43.100 //
gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇeneha nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  /
jñānato 'jñānato vāpi kāmato 'pi vā  // 2,43.101 //
gaṅgāyāṃ tu mṛto martyaḥ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ ca vindati  /
prāṇeṣūtsṛjyamāneṣu yo gaṅgāṃ saṃsmarennaraḥ  // 2,43.102 //
spṛśedvā pāpaśīlo 'pi sa vai yāti parāṃ gatim  // 2,43.103 //
gaṅgāṃ gatvā yaiḥ śarīraṃ visṛṣṭaṃ prāptā dhīrāste tu devaiḥ samatvam  /
tasmātsurvānprohya muktipradānvai sevedgaṅgāmā śarīrasya pātam  // 2,43.104 //
antarikṣe kṣitau toye pāpīyānapi yo mṛtaḥ  /
brahmaviṣṇuśivaiḥ pūjyaṃ padamakṣayyamaśnute  // 2,43.105 //
yo dharmiśṭaśca saprāṇaḥ prayataḥ śiṣṭasaṃmataḥ  /
cintayenmanasā gaṅgāṃ sa gatiṃ paramāṃ labhet  // 2,43.106 //
yatra tatra mṛto vāpi maraṇe samupasthite  /
bhaktyā gaṅgāṃ smaranyāti śaivaṃ vā vaiṣṇavaṃ puram  // 2,43.107 //
śaṃbhorjaṭākalāpāttu viniṣkrāntātikarkaśāt  /
plāvayitvā divaṃ ninye yā pāpānyagarātmajān  // 2,43.108 //
yāvantyasthīni gaṅgāyāṃ tiṣṭhanti puruṣasya vai  /
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate  // 2,43.109 //
gagātoye tu yasyāsthi nītvā prakṣipyate naraiḥ  /
tatkālamāditaḥ kṛtvā svargaloke bhavetsthitiḥ  // 2,43.110 //
gaṅgātoye tu yasyāsthi prāpyate śubhakarmaṇaḥ  /
na tasya punarāvṛttirbrahmalokātkathañcana  // 2,43.111 //
daśāhābhyantare yasya gaṅgātoye 'sthi saṃgatam  /
gaṅgāyāṃ maraṇe yādṛktādṛkphalamavāpnuyāt  // 2,43.112 //
snātvā tataḥ pañcagavyena siktvā hiraṇyamadhvājyatilairniyojya  /
tadasthipiṇḍaṃ puṭake nidhāya paśyan diśaṃ pretagaṇopagūḍhām  // 2,43.113 //
namo 'stu dharmāya vadanpraviśya jalaṃ sa me prīta iti kṣipecca  /
snātvā tatastīrthavaṭākṣayaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā pradadyādatha dakṣiṇāṃ tu  // 2,43.114 //
evaṃ kṛtvā pretapure sthitasya svarge gatiḥ syātta mahendratulyā  // 2,43.115 //
pravāhamavadhiṃ kṛtvā yāvaddhastacatuṣṭayam  /
tatra nārāyaṇaḥ svāmī nānyaḥ svāmī kadācana  // 2,43.116 //
na tatra pratigṛhṇīyātprāṇaiḥ kaṇṭhagatairapi  /
bhādraśuklacaturdaśyāṃ yāvadākramate jalam  // 2,43.117 //
tāvadgabhaṃ vijānīyāttaddūraṃ tīramucyate  /
sārddhahastaśataṃ yāvadgarbhastīraṃ tataḥ param  // 2,43.118 //
iti keṣāṃ mataṃ devi śrutismṛtiṣu saṃmatam  /
tīrādgavyūtimātraṃ tu paritaḥ kṣetramucyate  // 2,43.119 //
tīraṃ tyaktvā vasetkṣetre tīre vāso na ceṣyate  /
ekayojanavistīrṇā kṣetrasīmā taṭadvayāt  // 2,43.120 //
gaṅgāsīmāṃ na laghanti pāpānyapyakhilānyapi  /
tāṃ tu dṛṣṭvā palāyante yathā siṃhaṃ vanaukasaḥ  // 2,43.121 //
yatra gaṅgā mahābhāge rāmaśaṃbhutapovanam  /
siddhakṣetraṃ tu tajjñeyaṃ samantāttu triyojanam  // 2,43.122 //
tīrthe na pratigṛhṇīyātpuṇyeṣvāyataneṣu ca  /
nimitteṣu ca sarveṣu tannivṛtto bhavennaraḥ  // 2,43.123 //
tīrthe yaḥ pratigṛhṇāti puṇyeṣvāyataneṣu ca  /
niṣphalaṃ tasya tattīrthaṃ yāvattaddhanamucyate  // 2,43.124 //
gaṅgāvikrayāṇāddevi viṣṇorvikrayaṇaṃ bhavet  /
janārdane tu vikrīte vikrītaṃ bhuvanatrayam  // 2,43.125 //
gaṅgā tīrasamudbhūtāṃ ma-daṃ mūrghnā bibharti yaḥ  /
bibharti rūpaṃ sor'kasya tamonāśāya kevalam  // 2,43.126 //
gaṅgāpulinajāṃ dhūlimāstīryātha nijān pitṝn  /
prīṇayanyo naraḥ piṇḍāndadyāttān svarnayedapi  // 2,43.127 //
idaṃ te 'bhihitaṃ bhadre gaṅgāmāhātmyamuttamam  /
paṭhan śṛṇvannaro hyeti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  // 2,43.128 //
nityaṃ japyamidaṃ bhaktyā prayataiḥ śraddhayānvitaiḥ  /
vaiṣṇavīṃ gatimicchadbhiḥ śaivīṃ vā vidhinandini  // 2,43.129 //

iti śrībṛhannāradīyapurāṇottarabhāge mohinīvasusaṃvāde gaṅgāmāhātmye pūjādikathaṃ nāma tricatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
